        public static IEnumerable<Case> AllCases
        {
            get { return _allCases; }
        }

        public static IEnumerable<TestCaseData> AllCasesForExists
        {
            get { return HelpExtensions.SelectCasesForExistsFrom(_allCases); }
        }
